Memory bandwidth has always been a challenge for video cards, and that challenge only continues to get harder. Thanks to the mechanics of Moore‚Äôs Law, GPU transistor counts ‚Äì and therefore the quantities of various cores ‚Äì is growing at a rapid pace. Meanwhile DRAM, whose bandwidth is not subject to the same laws, has grown at a much smaller pace. The net result is that with nearly every generation, the amount of memory bandwidth available per FLOP, per texture lookup, and per pixel blend has continued to drop.

Is well read hyphenated

25 Feb 2024, 00:00

Should well written be hyphenated? If the term ‚Äúwell written‚Äù precedes the noun, it is a compound adjective and requires a comma: ‚ÄúIt is a well-written essay.‚Äù However, when it comes after the noun, no hyphen: ‚ÄúThe essay was well written.‚Äù Is well understood hyphenated? For example, a ‚Äúwell understood concept‚Äù is not hyphenated (well is an adverb modifying the adjective understood). Do you hyphenate well received? You use a hyphen when the adjective comes before the noun, not after it: It was a well-received show.
